msg:Don't worth the price
1. Hotel is old, TV is ridiculously small and you need to pay to watch a movie on it. Shampo and body wash is not one only use, is a big bottle that you share with who knows how many more people. 
2. Indoor pool is not for hotel guests is also part of a membership gym. If you are a foreigner the staff will behave like monkeys, looking at you, laughing... well he had to leave because that behaviour and the disgusting splits in the water from the members of the gym... but wear mask during the time you are leaving. Pool is cold, old and not comfortable.
3. Breakfast is okay, enough variety to have a 6, but quality is poor. Other 5 stars hotels like Hilton have very nice quality buffe food.
4. In from desk were in a panic attack... asking even for the stamp of our last entry in China... our check in took 3 times longer that the Chinese next to us, because of course for Chinese there is no need to know their last entry in China, just for foreigners.... racism? I don't know you might form your opinion.

Good points:
1. Bed is comfortable, room is spacious.
2. Next to the subway, few min by walking to some shopping malls.
It's absolutely not a 5 stars hotel, and there are nicer ones for the same price, even few hundreds more but you will see a drastic difference. Not recommended if you look to feel in a international 5 stars hotel, and enjoy the pool.

posted:Posted June 12, 2022
msg:The Sheraton is great. It's one of the few hotels in the city that I know I'll be attended to well. 

The location is very central in Futian district which allows for easy access to travel around the city. The staff at the front desk was friendly, fast and efficient. The entire check-in time took less than 10 minutes. 

Being in one of the Suites, you automatically gain access to the Sheraton Club Lounge for free dinner and drinks. One of the only complaints is it that the bar area should be kept neat and tidy and I'm also hoping that the Club lounge would be open for breakfast in the future. 

Breakfast was great and they have a wide selection to choose from. I had an order for coffee taken too and it was brought to the table in minutes. 

I'll definitely return again.

The hotel is located in the heart of Futian CBD. The subway station is located at the Exhibition Center Station, where Line 1 and Line 4 converge. The Futian High-speed Railway Station is within walking distance to the shopping park. Get out of Exit A1 and turn right back to reach the main entrance of the hotel. You will see a big Sheraton. The hotel is divided into east and west wings, and the guest room area is 11-24F in the west wing.
